[11/07/20, 11:54:19â€¯AM] Samir Arora-President- NAR ðŸ‡®ðŸ‡³: Friends
Times are not good and unfortunately Bengaluru is spiking on COVID cases. First and foremost, we request all our Members to take all safety precautions and wish each one of you and your families good health. Life will always be more important than Livelihood. Stay Safe, please.

The Economic outlook is confusing to say the least. Based on the feedback we have recieved, some of our members and some developers have done business exceedingly well in June. Kudos to them. 

Most members have done average business and are happy with survival at the moment.

Unfortunately, some members haven't been able to do business and obviously that adds to the Stress which is in any case amplified due to many issues COVID has caused. 

Some of us older people or/and high risk health people have gone into self lockdown compromising the business for survival.

As Jackma of Alibaba has said, Survive 2020 and you are already Profitable. 

In these unique and trying circumstances, it is easy to lose cool, not think rationally, feel edgy and irritated and sometimes let out the frustration on others, may it be colleagues or family. The mental balance & Positive thoughts, however will be the most important tool to battle any Negative circumstances around us and we all have to stand together, united as One at CREA (I) in these pandemic ridden circumstances.The Times are Testing but Together we can stand to the Test of Times and face challenges together to emerge victorius.

This is the time to handhold each member. Each one of us in small groups can be a support system to each other in multiple ways. 

The Committee at CREA (I) is all Members like you. Each one faced with their own challenges, like you. However, we are trying our best to come out with Innovative Ideas to help all Members sail through these times. The Developers have same story. Some have done well, Most par average and Many down. We are all a part of the Eco system and this is the time for all of us to come up with innovative ideas and build a support system exactly like a family and we at CREA (I) are a family. ðŸ™

The Committee will work on concern areas expressed by some members surely but we also request innovative ideas, value add suggestions and a support system to ensure we sail through this phase with least hiccups. There is no miracle yet, either to handle COVID or the issues it has thrown up but Positive attitude and spirit, can help each member make CREA (I) worthy of it being called the Best till now.

Together, with compassion and care lets create a support system and try to help all our members do some transactions to enable all sail through this diffult phase of life. This Too Shall Pass.

Once again, Stay Safe.
Best wishes always,

Samir Arora
Proud Member &
President CREA (I)
